      <div class="post-1992 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-uncategorized" id="post-1992">
       <h1 class="entry-title">
        Country Living Shrinky Dinks Jewelry
       </h1>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="entry-date">
         Thursday, February 10, 2011
        </span>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="https://www.google.com/+CatheHolden?rel=author" target="_blank" title="More from Cathe Holden">
          Cathe Holden
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>
         Ive been beyond excited about the new March issue of
         <a href="http://www.countryliving.com/">
          Country Living magazine
         </a>
         coming out this week! I, along with three other DIY bloggers, was asked to share a craft project with their readers. (Uhhm, twist my arm!) If you are a new visitor of JSIM,
         <em>
          <strong>
           Welcome!
          </strong>
         </em>
         <a href="http://www.countryliving.com/crafts/projects/how-to-make-a-shriky-dink-bracelet">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2023" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/CHCountryLiving3-11.jpg" height="401" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="CHCountryLiving3-11" width="334"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2023" height="401" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/CHCountryLiving3-11.jpg" title="CHCountryLiving3-11" width="334"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         They favored
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/2010/05/fun-with-shrink-plastic-blog-ring/">
          a past Shrinky Dinks project
         </a>
         I posted on my blog so I created a special craft just for the March issue and included free digital images for you to download from the
         <a href="http://www.countryliving.com/crafts/projects/how-to-make-a-shriky-dink-bracelet">
          Country Living website
         </a>
         .
         <a href="http://www.countryliving.com/crafts/projects/how-to-make-a-shriky-dink-bracelet">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1990" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/JSIMcl1.jpg" height="339" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="JSIMcl1" width="339"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1990" height="339" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/JSIMcl1.jpg" title="JSIMcl1" width="339"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         The images are modified scans of vintage flea market ephemera Ive collected, most of which Ive shared with you on my blog.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrinkephemera.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1977" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrinkephemera.jpg" height="270" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="shrinkephemera" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1977" height="270" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrinkephemera.jpg" title="shrinkephemera" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         Once the images are
         <a href="http://www.countryliving.com/crafts/projects/how-to-make-a-shriky-dink-bracelet">
          downloaded
         </a>
         , (dont worry that they look faded, they will burst with color once baked), print to 8 x 10
         <a href="http://www.shrinkydinks.com">
          Shrinky Dinks sheets
          <em>
           made specifically for ink jet printers
          </em>
         </a>
         . Before printing, however, you can personalize some of the images digitally or by hand.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink1.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1985" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink1.jpg" height="310" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="shrink1" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1985" height="310" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink1.jpg" title="shrink1" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Trim out the individual pieces.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink2.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1984" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink2.jpg" height="302" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="shrink2" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1984" height="302" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink2.jpg" title="shrink2" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         If creating a linking bracelet, punch two holes- one on each side of the images you want to link. I use a 1/8 punch. It might be a good idea to make a few more than you think you will need for a bracelet so you can adjust the length of the bracelet if needed. If you are making charms to hang from a necklace chain, punch one hole each in either the top or side of the images.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink3.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1983" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink3.jpg" height="308" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="shrink3" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1983" height="308" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink3.jpg" title="shrink3" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         Bake as directed to shrink the images. I only bake two at a time because theres a chance that if you  have too many in your oven at once they may curl into one another and  stick while baking. Its fun to watch them distort while baking only to lay completely flat when done.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink4.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1982" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink4.jpg" height="223" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="shrink4" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1982" height="223" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink4.jpg" title="shrink4" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Once cooled, spray the charms with a clear acrylic to keep any ink from bleeding. Link the charms together with jump rings to make a bracelet.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink6.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1981" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink6.jpg" height="297" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="shrink6" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1981" height="297" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink6.jpg" title="shrink6" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Finish with a toggle or clasp.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink7.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1978" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink7.jpg" height="156" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="shrink7" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1978" height="156" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink7.jpg" title="shrink7" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         If making a necklace, lay out your charms in the order you want them to hang from the chain, then begin adding charms with jump rings working from the center out towards the ends of the chain.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink8.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1980" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink8.jpg" height="291" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="shrink8" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1980" height="291" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink8.jpg" title="shrink8" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink9.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1979" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink9.jpg" height="275" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="shrink9" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1979" height="275" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/shrink9.jpg" title="shrink9" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         Finish the necklace with a toggle or clasp set.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimshrinkplate.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2004" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimshrinkplate.jpg" height="470" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="jsimshrinkplate" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2004" height="470" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimshrinkplate.jpg" title="jsimshrinkplate" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/JSIMcl2.jpg">
          <br/>
         </a>
         I personalized some of the charms on my necklace. An enveloped addressed to my sister Jennifer, because shes always been so thoughtful to send me letters to me.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl3.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1988" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl3.jpg" height="255" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="jsimcl3" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1988" height="255" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl3.jpg" title="jsimcl3" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         An ID card.
         <em>
          (Not my real address.)
         </em>
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl4.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1987" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl4.jpg" height="283" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="jsimcl4" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1987" height="283" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl4.jpg" title="jsimcl4" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         A personal calling card.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl5.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1986" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl5.jpg" height="323" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="jsimcl5" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1986" height="323" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl5.jpg" title="jsimcl5" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         A little name label for me and Mr. Wonderful.
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl11.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1993" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl11.jpg" height="325" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="jsimcl11" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1993" height="325" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl11.jpg" title="jsimcl11" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl10.jpg">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1975" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl10.jpg" height="326" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="jsimcl10" width="470"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1975" height="326" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/jsimcl10.jpg" title="jsimcl10" width="470"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         The makers of Shrinky Dinks has a wonderful exclusive offer just for JSIM readers!
         <a href="http://shrinkydinks.com/">
         </a>
         <a href="http://shrinkydinks.com">
          <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2082" data-lazy-src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/JSIM4FREE1.jpg" height="401" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/plugins/lazy-load/images/1x1.trans.gif" title="JSIM4FREE" width="406"/>
          <noscript>
           <img alt="" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-2082" height="401" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-content/uploads/JSIM4FREE1.jpg" title="JSIM4FREE" width="406"/>
          </noscript>
         </a>
         <em>
          <strong>
           Any
          </strong>
         </em>
         size order using the discount code
         <strong>
          <span style="color: #ff0000;">
           JSIM4FREE
          </span>
         </strong>
         gets you a fun, FREE gift! Simply go to their website,
         <a href="http://shrinkydinks.com/">
          <strong>
           ShrinkyDinks.com
          </strong>
         </a>
         , click on the
         <strong>
          Shop On Line
         </strong>
         button to get to their store. Enter the code in the discount code section at checkout.
        </p>
        <p>
         Oh, and youll want to bookmark these fabulous DIY blogs featured in the same Country Living Idea Notebook!
        </p>
        <p>
         
         <a href="http://cfabbridesigns.com/blog/">
          Camilla Fabbri  cfabbridesigns.com/blog
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         
         <a href="http://papernstitchblog.com/">
          Brittni Mehlhoff  papernstitchblog.com
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         
         <a href="http://katepruitt.com/">
          Kate Pruitt  katepruitt.com
         </a>
        </p>
        <p class="no-break">

I usually just rubber stamp or draw on the shrink because I have not found a computer shrink I like.  I will buy the Country Living magazine to see what kind you have used .  Again Thank You for sharing.

            <!-- .comment-author .vcard -->
            <div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
             <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/2011/02/country-living-shrinky-dink-jewelry/#comment-25155">
              February 11, 2011 at 10:04 am
             </a>
            </div>
            <!-- .comment-meta .commentmetadata -->
            <div class="comment-body">
             <p>
              Hi Teresa.
             </p>
             <p>
              If you have software that works with layers, that is a good way to add text. Other suggestions are to open the file within your software, or place the file within your software. If either of those work, use your text tool to type names, etc. OR, save file as a JPG and use it as a positioning image for typing onto. Then remove the jpg image before printing. Print the original PDF file, then run back through your printer again and print the text section. Be sure to practice with paper first before using up your printable shrinky sheets. Hope that helps.
             </p>
            </div>

          <div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">

            February 18, 2011 at 10:21 am
           </a>
          </div>
          <!-- .comment-meta .commentmetadata -->
          <div class="comment-body">
           <p>
            Thank you!  I had to get right to making this.  I did a necklace, bracelet and earrings.  Id done a few dozen 68 watercolors about 10 years ago and scanned them.  So I used these images to make the set and its colorful and fun looking!  Wore it yesterday and got lots of compliments.  It was my test set.  I intend to make a few as gifts for girlfriends.  See my Facebook page for photos of this set:  Facebook.com/marcy.brennan
           </p>
           <p>
            Just one question:  Im using the ink jet shrinky dinks.  Sometimes the little tiles turn over revealing the plain white side (reverse side of the image).  Its kind of ugly to see.  Any idea if the reverse side will take acrylic paint or stamping, etc?  I looked at the Shrinky Dink site and it didnt address that question.  Thanks so much!! What a fun project.
           </p>
          </div>

              March 6, 2011 at 9:31 pm

            </div>
            <!-- .comment-meta .commentmetadata -->
            <div class="comment-body">
             <p>
              Hi Judy, The images you see are on an 8 x 10 sheet of inkjet Shrinky Dinks. The individual charm sizes vary. A good rule of thumb is to make the originals 3 times larger than you want the finished pieces to be. Its not an exact science, but thats a good rule of thumb.
             </p>
            </div>

           <p>
            Hi Cathe,
            <br/>
            I have been waiting forever to try this project. The Shrinky dink supplies were out at the craft store for a long time so I think everyone read your great idea at once. I finally got the shrinky dink paper made for ink jets, found an ink jet printer that would work, had someone print them for me and then went to work. All of my charms are dark and dingy, almost burnt looking. I dont think it is the heat as I tried different ones at 300, 325, and 350. I think it may be something I am doing wrong with the printer. Does the lighting need to be changed or brightened before printing them up? I wasnt there when they were printed so I dont think she darkened them or adjusted anything else. I am going to try again tomorrow at a different friends home. I am running out of time as I had bought all these wonderful supplies to make my girlfriend a birthday gift. I only have 36 hours left. EeeeK! Does anyone know what could be going wrong? Thanks so much,
            <br/>
            Crystal

            <!-- .comment-author .vcard -->
            <div class="comment-meta commentmetadata">
             <a href="http://justsomethingimade.com/2011/02/country-living-shrinky-dink-jewelry/#comment-27968">
              April 1, 2011 at 8:23 am
             </a>
            </div>
            <!-- .comment-meta .commentmetadata -->
            <div class="comment-body">
             <p>
              Troubleshooting:
             </p>
             <p>
              Be careful not to bake too long. Despite the SD instructions, I bake mine for around 15 seconds, or until the stop distorting and lie flat. The second they flatten I pull them out. Your colors will tend to brown if you keep them in too long. As far as how much to screen back, you may need to try different levels of screening. Print only a couple of photos at once to one end of your sheet of SD and test. Then you have the rest of the sheet to work with. I am really sorry to hear you have been having trouble. Be sure you are using SD for inkjet printers.
             </p>
            </div>

            I have to tell youI was looking through Country Living at my moms house (a  magazine subscription that she has because of my childrens mad fundraising skills) and I came across this Shrinky Dink bracelet. I LOVED shrinky dinks when I was a kid (I am 33 now) and although I am not quite sure what we did with them, they were so much fun. Anyway, I made these today with a friend for Mothers Day presents, a birthday present, and one for me
            <img alt=":)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://justsomethingimade.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/icon_smile.gif"/>

          Hi, Im Cathe (pronounced the same as Cathy). Im a graphic designer, crafter, creative blogger, &amp; flea market enthusiast. I live just north of San Francisco in lovely Petaluma, California with my husband, Mr. Wonderful &amp; our 3 awesome teenagers.
